The most popular of these companions is Churchill the Bulldog, a lovable new furry companion similar to Dogmeat in the base game. Churchill is named after Winston Churchill, the famous Prime Minister of the UK.\n\nChurchill is one of the first companions you can meet while exploring apocalyptic London. He's the perfect dose of British charm to liven up the wasteland, and while players have reported a bug that traps Churchill after you dismiss him, you can avoid that fate by keeping Churchill at your side.\n\nRelated\n\nFallout London Finally Releases With New Story, Environments, & Characters\n\nAfter years of development and several major setbacks, the long-awaited Fallout: London mod is finally here and it's everything Team FOLON promised.\n\nWhere To Find & Recruit Churchill\n\nFind Him Near The Factory\n\nAfter installing Fallout London and some city exploration, you should make your way toward the Prilladog Food Factory. This factory can be found near the center of the city map, along the southern shore of the Thames. You should pass by the building while journeying to Thameshaven. When you arrive there, you will see Churchill fighting off a pack of stray dogs. It's time to jump to the rescue of your new furry friend and kill the strays.\n\nWith Churchill safe, head to the entrance of Prilladog Food Factory, where you can talk to a Factory Guard. Regardless of how you respond to him, he will offer to give you Churchill. By accepting his offer, you can speak to Churchill like any other companion and invite him to travel with you. With that, you have a lovable and loyal guard dog at your side.\n\nWhat Can Churchill Do As A Companion?\n\nHow To Protect Churchill\n\nOnce Churchill is at your side and ready to explore the wasteland in Fallout: London, he will behave like many other companions. When you ask him to follow you, he will stay by your side and join you wherever you go. If you're worried about bringing him somewhere dangerous, you can also ask him to stay put. When you need to offload some of your loot, you can trade with Churchill, allowing him to carry some of your items for a while.\n\nOne of the biggest let-downs of Fallout: London is that you cannot actually pet Churchill.\n\nAs a dog, Churchill is able to find loot and enemies, similar to Dogmeat in Fallout 4. The game will let you know when Churchill has found something of interest and may lead you to the goods. Finally, when you enter combat, Churchill will help you fight off enemies, but be careful! If he goes down, he will need a stimpak to get him up and at it again. Fairly soon after leaving Vault 111, the Sole Survivor will be tasked with defending themselves against all manner of mutated creatures including Radroaches and Bloatflies, yet some of the most annoying are Mole rats. These fleshy abominations can deliver a terrifying chomp if they get too close and they have the added ability of tunnelling away from danger, making them difficult to pin down.\n\nYet as it turns out, Mole Rats are even more disturbing than many players may have expected as revealed in this Reddit post by MysteriousPudding175 wherein it's proved that the mutated mammals actually have two sets of teeth.\n\nWhile most will likely already be familiar with the massive set of incisors that it uses to attack its prey, behind them is a different set of what appear to be molars used to crunch and chomp particular tough food. A Glowing Mole Rat can be annoying for those who don't want to deal with an increase in their rad level but arguably the most annoying variant is the Rabid Mole Rat. This critter comes equipped with a poison-like ability that can deal damage over time, meaning the Sole Survivor will want to put down these beasts from as far away as possible.\n\nYet the most dangerous form of Mole Rat in Fallout 4 is undoubtedly the \"Suicide\" variant which charges at the player with a set of fragmentation mines strapped to its back. When they get too close, the explosives detonate, destroying the carrier but also unleashing a severe amount of damage on anyone and anything in the vicinity. It's unclear who's setting up the Mole Rats for such a vicious demise but it's presumed that Raiders are responsible.\n\nWhatever form the Mole Rat may take in Fallout 4, the radioactive creatures are some of the most iconic enemies in the entire franchise. While they may not have the imposing power of a Radscorpion or a Death Claw, there's just something fun about gunning down a pack of them in quick succession. One such sidequest is \"Catching Up\", a fairly short jaunt to a nearby library on behalf of \"Sabertooth\" Syd. Syd wants to learn how to read and tasks you with grabbing some kids books from the library, and if you can find his childhood favorite: Dove's Dilemma, then that would be perfect.\n\nFallout London does a surprisingly good job of hiding that particular book, however, stashing it under a box in an easy-to-miss part of the library. This guide will explain how to start Syd's quest, how to get into the section of the library where the children's books are kept, and how to find a copy of Dove's Dilemma.\n\nRelated\n\nHow to Play Fallout London on Steam & GOG\n\nFallout London is an amazing mod for Fallout 4, but it can be tricky to get working. Here's how to install and play the mod.\n\nHow to Start Catching Up\n\nThe Catching Up Quest can be accessed at any point after you protect the Swan and Mitre and take out the scout that escaped. Once you've done this, just speak to \"Sabertooth\" Syd in the Swan and Mitre to learn about his plan and start the quest. He'll point you towards the Churchill Library to hunt down the books, which is thankfully only a short walk away.\n\nHow to Get into the Library's Right Wing\n\nTo get into the part of the library where the Children's Books are kept, you'll need to head up to the top floor first. The Chief Librarian's Office is up here, with a key to the Book Room lying on their desk. Open the door to their office while standing to one side of the door, since it's rigged up to a shotgun trap. After you get inside, you can steal the shotgun for personal use, along with anything else that isn't nailed down.\n\nSnag the Key from the Director's Desk and check the terminal to learn a bit more about how the library has been operating. That secure room of banned books sounds interesting, but it's unlikely to contain Dove's Dilemma. With this key we can now open the door to Churchill Library Right Wing, which can be found on the same floor you entered on. This section of the Library is where we'll find the Kid's Books Syd wants.\n\nHow to Find Dove's Dilemma\n\nClose\n\nYou'll see a ramp ahead once you enter the Right Wing. Take out the incoming Ghouls and then use that ramp to get upstairs. Turn around at the top of the ramp and look for a cardboard box on top of a shelf. Pick up the cardboard box by holding down E while looking at it, then move it somewhere else to reveal Dove's Dilemma hidden underneath it. Grab this book, then pick up some more kid's books from this library section to round out the collection you're giving to Syd. Once you've got four books you can head back to Syd and complete the quest.\n\nFallout 4\n\nRPG\n\nAction\n\nSystems\n\nOpenCritic Reviews Top Critic Rating:87/100 Critics Recommend:89%\n\nFranchise
